lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">与其他信息相关的审计报告的参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 28.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.55pt">参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">：当注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取所有其他信息，且未识别出其他信息存在重大错报时，适用于任何被审计单位，无论</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">是上市实体还是非上市实体的无保留意见审计报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 28.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.55pt">参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">：当注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取部分其他信息，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">且未识别出其他信息存在重大错报，并预期能够在审计报告日后获取</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">剩余其他信息时，适用于上市实体的无保留意见审计报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 28.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.55pt">参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">：当注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取部分其他信息，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">且未识别出其他信息存在重大错报，并预期能够在审计报告日后获取</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">剩余其他信息时，适用于非上市实体的无保留意见审计报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 28.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.55pt">参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">：当注册会计师在审计报告日前未获取任何其他信息，但预期能够在审计报告日后获取其他信息时，适用于上市实体的无保</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">留意见审计报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 28.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.55pt">参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">：当注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取所有其他信息，并且已确定其他信息存在重大错报时，适用于任何被审计单位，无论</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">是上市实体还是非上市实体的无保留意见审计报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 28.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.55pt">参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">：当注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取所有其他信息，</SPAN>但合并财务报表重要项目的审计范围受到限制，且影响其他信息时，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">适用于任何被审计单位，无论是上市实体还是非上市实体的保留意见</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">审计报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 28.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.55pt">参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">：当注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取所有其他信息，</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">且对合并财务报表发表的否定意见也对其他信息有影响时，适用于任</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">何被审计单位，无论是上市实体还是非上市实体的否定意见审计报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.8pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>1</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">：当注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取所有其他信息，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">且未识别出其他信息存在重大错报时，适用于任何被审计单位，无论</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">是上市实体还是非上市实体的无保留意见审计报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>背景信息：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>．对上市实体或非上市实体整套财务报表进行审计。该审计不<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">属于集团审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">即不适用《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1401</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">对集团财务报表审计的特殊考虑》</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>．管理层按照企业会计准则编制财务报表；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">．审计业务约定条款体现了《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1111</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>就审计业务约定条款达成一致意见》中关于管理层对财务报表<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">责任的描述；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>．基于获取的审计证据，注册会计师认为发表无保留意见是恰当的；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>．适用的相关职业道德要求为中国注册会计师职业道德守则；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 15.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -2.6pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">．基于获取的审计证据，根据《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1324</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">持续经营》，注册会计师认为可能导致对被审计单位持续经营</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">能力产生重大疑虑的事项或情况不存在重大不确定性；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">．已按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>在审计报告<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">中沟通关键审计事项》的规定沟通了关键审计事项；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>8</SPAN>．注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取所有其他信息，且未识别出信息存在重大错报；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9</SPAN>．负责监督财务报表的人员与负责编制财务报表的人员不同；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">．除财务报表审计外，注册会计师还承担法律法规要求的其他</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">报告责任，且注册会计师决定在审计报告中履行其他报告责任。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">审计报告</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>股份有限公司全体股东：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%"><FONT 
size=4>一、对财务报表出具的审计报告</FONT></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -6.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-width: 95%; mso-text-raise: 6.5pt'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt"><FONT face=微软雅黑><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-font-width: 95%">（一）审计意见</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt">我们审计了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">股份有限公司</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">以下简称</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">公司</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">财务报表，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">包括</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">日的资产负债表，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">年度的利润表、现金流</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">量表、股东权益变动表以及相关财务报表附注。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">我们认为，后附的财务报表在所有重大方面按照企业会计准则的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.15pt">规定编制，公允反映了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">公司</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">日的财务状况以及</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>20</FONT></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>年度的经营成果和现金流量。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>（二）形成审计意见的基础<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">我们按照中国注册会计师审计准则的规定执行了审计工作。审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt">报告的</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt"><FONT face=微软雅黑>注册会计师对财务报表审计的责任</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">部分进一步阐述了我们</SPAN>在这些准则下的责任。按照中国注册会计师职业道德守则，我们独立<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.35pt">于</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">公司，并履行了职业道德方面的其他责任。我们相信，我们获取的审计证据是充分、适当的，为发表审计意见提供了基础。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%"><FONT 
size=4>（三）关键审计事项</FONT></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -6.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-width: 95%; mso-text-raise: 6.5pt'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>关键审计事项是我们根据职业判断，认为对本期财务报表审计最<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26pt"><o:wrapblock><v:line


strokeweight=".16936mm"><w:wrap type="topAndBottom" 
anchorx="page"></w:wrap></v:line></o:wrapblock><BR style="mso-ignore: vglayout" 
clear=all><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 11.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: 3.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-text-raise: -3.5pt">如果审计报告中不包含<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>“</SPAN>按照相关法律法规的要求报告的事项<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>”</SPAN>部分，则不需要加入此标题。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 6pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -4pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-text-raise: 4.0pt'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">本段适用于按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>在审计报告中沟通关键审计事项》的规定沟通关键审计事项的情形。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">为重要的事项。这些事项的应对以对财务报表整体进行审计并形成审</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">计意见为背景，我们不对这些事项单独发表意见。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">在审计报告中沟</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">通关键审计事项》的规定描述每一关键审计事项。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">（四）其他信息</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>公司管理层（以下简称管理层）对其他信息负责。其他信息包括<SPAN 
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[X</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">报告中涵盖的信息，但不包括财务报表和我们的审计报告</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.4pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">我们对财务报表发表的审计意见不涵盖其他信息，我们也不对其</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">他信息发表任何形式的鉴证结论。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>结合我们对财务报表的审计，我们的责任是阅读其他信息，在此<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">过程中，考虑其他信息是否与财务报表或我们在审计过程中了解到的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">情况存在重大不一致或者似乎存在重大错报。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT 
size=4>基于我们已执行的工作，如果我们确定其他信息存在重大错报，我们应当报告该事实。在这方面，我们无任何事项需要报告。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">（五）管理层和治理层对财务报表的责任</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1501</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">对财务报表形成审计意见和出具审计报告》的规定报告，见《</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&lt;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">中国注册会计师审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1501</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>对财务报表形成审计意见和出具审计报告<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&gt;</SPAN>应用<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">指南》参考格式</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US

style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US

</SPAN></SPAN>（签名并盖<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">章</SPAN>）<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">中</SPAN>国注册会<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">计</SPAN>师：</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×××</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>（签名并盖章）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>中国</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>××</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>市<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US

<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 16.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">计意见和出具审计报告</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&gt;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">应用指南》参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: 3.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-text-raise: -3.5pt">披露项目合伙人姓名的要求仅适用于上市实体。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>2</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">：当注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取部分其他信息，且</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">未识别出其他信息存在重大错报，并预期能够在审计报告日后获取剩</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">余其他信息时，适用于上市实体的无保留意见审计报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>背景信息：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>．对上市实体整套财务报表进行审计。该审计不属于集团审计<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>（<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">即不适用《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1401</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">对集团财务报</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.95pt">表审计的特殊考虑》</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>．管理层按照企业会计准则编制财务报表；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">．审计业务约定条款体现了《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1111</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>就审计业务约定条款达成一致意见》中关于管理层对财务报表<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">责任的描述；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>．基于获取的审计证据，注册会计师认为发表无保留意见是恰当的；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>．适用的相关职业道德要求为中国注册会计师职业道德守则；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 15.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -2.6pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">．基于获取的审计证据，根据《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1324</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">持续经营》，注册会计师认为可能导致对被审计单位持续经营</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">能力产生重大疑虑的事项或情况不存在重大不确定性；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">．已按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>在审计报告<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">中沟通关键审计事项》的规定沟通了关键审计事项；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>8</SPAN>．注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取部分其他信息，且未识别<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">出信息存在重大错报，并预期能够在审计报告日后获取剩余其他信息；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9</SPAN>．负责监督财务报表的人员与负责编制财务报表的人员不同；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">．除财务报表审计外，注册会计师还承担法律法规要求的其他</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">报告责任，且注册会计师决定在审计报告中履行其他报告责任。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">审计报告</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>股份有限公司全体股东：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%"><FONT 
size=4>一、对财务报表出具的审计报告</FONT></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -6.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-width: 95%; mso-text-raise: 6.5pt'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt"><FONT face=微软雅黑><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-font-width: 95%">（一）审计意见</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt">我们审计了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">股份有限公司</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">以下简称</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">公司</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">财务报表，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">包括</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">日的资产负债表，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">年度的利润表、现金流</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">量表、股东权益变动表以及相关财务报表附注。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">我们认为，后附的财务报表在所有重大方面按照企业会计准则的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.15pt">规定编制，公允反映了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">公司</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">日的财务状况以及</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>20</FONT></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>年度的经营成果和现金流量。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>（二）形成审计意见的基础<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">我们按照中国注册会计师审计准则的规定执行了审计工作。审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt">报告的</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt"><FONT face=微软雅黑>注册会计师对财务报表审计的责任</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">部分进一步阐述了我们</SPAN>在这些准则下的责任。按照中国注册会计师职业道德守则，我们独立<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.35pt">于</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">公司，并履行了职业道德方面的其他责任。我们相信，我们获取的审计证据是充分、适当的，为发表审计意见提供了基础。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">（三）关键审计事项</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>关键审计事项是我们根据职业判断，认为对本期财务报表审计最<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">为重要的事项。这些事项的应对以对财务报表整体进行审计并形成审</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">计意见为背景，我们不对这些事项单独发表意见。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>


strokeweight=".48pt"><w:wrap type="topAndBottom" 
anchorx="page"></w:wrap></v:line></o:wrapblock><BR style="mso-ignore: vglayout" 
clear=all><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">在审计报告中沟</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">通关键审计事项》的规定描述每一关键审计事项。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: 3.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-text-raise: -3.5pt">如果审计报告中不包含<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>“</SPAN>按照相关法律法规的要求报告的事项<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>”</SPAN>部分，则不需要加入此标题。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">（四）其他信息</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>公司管理层（以下简称管理层）对其他信息负责。其他信<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">息包括</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>X</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">报告</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">但不包括财务报表和我们的审计报告）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.15pt">和</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>Y</SPAN>报告。<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">我们在审计报告日前已获取</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>X</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">报告，而</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>Y</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">报告预期将在审计报告日后提供给我们。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">我们对财务报表发表的审计意见不涵盖其他信息，我们也不对其</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">他信息发表任何形式的鉴证结论。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>结合我们对财务报表的审计，我们的责任是阅读其他信息，在此<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">过程中，考虑其他信息是否与财务报表或我们在审计过程中了解到的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">情况存在重大不一致或者似乎存在重大错报。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">基于我们对审计报告日前获取的其他信息已执行的工作，如果我</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">们确定其他信息存在重大错报，我们应当报告该事实。在这方面，我</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">们无任何事项需要报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">当我们阅读</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>Y</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">报告后，如果确定其中存在重大错报，审计准则要求我们与治理层沟通该事项并采取</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">描述适用的措施</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -6.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-text-raise: 6.5pt'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">（五）管理层和治理层对财务报表的责任</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN

face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">对财务报表形成审计意见和出具审计报告》的规定报告，见《</SPAN><SPAN

<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>3</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">：当注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取部分其他信息，且</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">未识别出其他信息存在重大错报，并预期能够在审计报告日后获取剩</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">余其他信息时，适用于非上市实体的无保留意见审计报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>背景信息：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>．对非上市实体整套财务报表进行审计。该审计不属于集团审计（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">即不适用《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1401</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">对集团财务</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">报表审计的特殊考虑》</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>．管理层按照企业会计准则编制财务报表；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">．审计业务约定条款体现了《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1111</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>就审计业务约定条款达成一致意见》中关于管理层对财务报表<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">责任的描述；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>．基于获取的审计证据，注册会计师认为发表无保留意见是恰当的；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>．适用的相关职业道德要求为中国注册会计师职业道德守则；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 15.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -2.6pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">．基于获取的审计证据，根据《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1324</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">持续经营》，注册会计师认为可能导致对被审计单位持续经营</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">能力产生重大疑虑的事项或情况不存在重大不确定性；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN>．注册会计师未被要求，并且也决定不沟通关键审计事项；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>8</SPAN>．注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取部分其他信息，且未识别<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">出信息存在重大错报，并预期能够在审计报告日后获取剩余其他信息；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9</SPAN>．负责监督财务报表的人员与负责编制财务报表的人员不同；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">．除财务报表审计外，注册会计师不承担法律法规要求的其他</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">报告责任。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">审计报告</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>股份有限公司全体股东：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>一、审计意见<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt">我们审计了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">股份有限公司</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">以下简称</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">公司</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">财务报表，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">包括</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">日的资产负债表，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">年度的利润表、现金流</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">量表、股东权益变动表以及相关财务报表附注。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">我们认为，后附的财务报表在所有重大方面按照企业会计准则的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.15pt">规定编制，公允反映了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">公司</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">日的财务状况以及</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>20</FONT></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>年度的经营成果和现金流量。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">二、形成审计意见的基础</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">我们按照中国注册会计师审计准则的规定执行了审计工作。审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt">报告的</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt"><FONT face=微软雅黑>注册会计师对财务报表审计的责任</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">部分进一步阐述了我们</SPAN>在这些准则下的责任。按照中国注册会计师职业道德守则，我们独立<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.35pt">于</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">公司，并履行了职业道德方面的其他责任。我们相信，我们获取的审计证据是充分、适当的，为发表审计意见提供了基础。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>三、其他信息<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>公司管理层（以下简称管理层）对其他信息负责。我们在审计报告日前已获取的其他信息包括<SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[X</SPAN>报告中涵盖的信息，但不包括财务报表和我们的审计报告<SPAN 
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.4pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">我们对财务报表发表的审计意见不涵盖其他信息，我们也不对其</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">他信息发表任何形式的鉴证结论。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>结合我们对财务报表的审计，我们的责任是阅读其他信息，在此<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">过程中，考虑其他信息是否与财务报表或我们在审计过程中了解到的</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>情况存在重大不一致或者似乎存在重大错报。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">基于我们对审计报告日前获取的其他信息已执行的工作，如果我</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">们确定其他信息存在重大错报，我们应当报告该事实。在这方面，我</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">们无任何事项需要报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">四、管理层和治理层对财务报表的责任</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1501</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">对财务报表形成审计意见和出具审计报告》的规定报告，见《</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&lt;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">中国注册会计师审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1501</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>对财务报表形成审计意见和出具审计报告<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&gt;</SPAN>应用<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">指南》参考格式</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">五、注册会计师对财务报表审计的责任</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1501</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">对财务报表形成审计意见和出具审计报告》的规定报告，见《</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&lt;</SPAN><SPAN

</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US

face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US

style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><SPAN

face=微软雅黑>日<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>4</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">：当注册会计师在审计报告日前未获取任何其他信息，但</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">预期能够在审计报告日后获取其他信息时，适用于上市实体的无保留</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">意见审计报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>背景信息：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>．对上市实体整套财务报表进行审计。该审计不属于集团审计<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>（<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">即不适用《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1401</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">对集团财务报</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.95pt">表审计的特殊考虑》</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>．管理层按照企业会计准则编制财务报表；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">．审计业务约定条款体现了《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1111</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>就审计业务约定条款达成一致意见》中关于管理层对财务报表<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">责任的描述；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>．基于获取的审计证据，注册会计师认为发表无保留意见是恰当的；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>．适用的相关职业道德要求为中国注册会计师职业道德守则；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 15.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -2.6pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">．基于获取的审计证据，根据《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1324</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">持续经营》，注册会计师认为可能导致对被审计单位持续经营</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">能力产生重大疑虑的事项或情况不存在重大不确定性；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">．已按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>在审计报告<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">中沟通关键审计事项》的规定沟通了关键审计事项；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>8</SPAN>．注册会计师在审计报告日前未获取任何其他信息，但预期能够在审计报告日后获取其他信息；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9</SPAN>．负责监督财务报表的人员与负责编制财务报表的人员不同；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">．除财务报表审计外，注册会计师还承担法律法规要求的其他</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">报告责任，且注册会计师决定在审计报告中履行其他报告责任。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">审计报告</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>股份有限公司全体股东：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%"><FONT 
size=4>一、对财务报表出具的审计报告</FONT></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -6.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-width: 95%; mso-text-raise: 6.5pt'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt"><FONT face=微软雅黑><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-font-width: 95%">（一）审计意见</SPAN></B><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt">我们审计了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">股份有限公司</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">以下简称</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">公司</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">财务报表，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">包括</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">日的资产负债表，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">年度的利润表、现金流</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">量表、股东权益变动表以及相关财务报表附注。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">我们认为，后附的财务报表在所有重大方面按照企业会计准则的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.15pt">规定编制，公允反映了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">公司</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">日的财务状况以及</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>20</FONT></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>年度的经营成果和现金流量。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>（二）形成审计意见的基础<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">我们按照中国注册会计师审计准则的规定执行了审计工作。审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt">报告的</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt"><FONT face=微软雅黑>注册会计师对财务报表审计的责任</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">部分进一步阐述了我们</SPAN>在这些准则下的责任。按照中国注册会计师职业道德守则，我们独立<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.35pt">于</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">公司，并履行了职业道德方面的其他责任。我们相信，我们获取的审计证据是充分、适当的，为发表审计意见提供了基础。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">（三）关键审计事项</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>关键审计事项是我们根据职业判断，认为对本期财务报表审计最<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">为重要的事项。这些事项的应对以对财务报表整体进行审计并形成审</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">计意见为背景，我们不对这些事项单独发表意见。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26pt"><o:wrapblock><v:line


strokeweight=".48pt"><w:wrap type="topAndBottom" 
anchorx="page"></w:wrap></v:line></o:wrapblock><BR style="mso-ignore: vglayout" 
clear=all><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">在审计报告中沟</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">通关键审计事项》的规定描述每一关键审计事项。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: 3.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-text-raise: -3.5pt">如果审计报告中不包含<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>“</SPAN>按照相关法律法规的要求报告的事项<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>”</SPAN>部分，则不需要加入此标题。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">（四）其他信息</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>公司管理层（以下简称管理层）对其他信息负责。其他信息包括<SPAN 
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[X</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">报告中涵盖的信息，但不包括财务报表和我们的审计报告</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>X</SPAN>报告预期将在审计报告日后提供给我们。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">我们对财务报表发表的审计意见不涵盖其他信息，我们也不对其</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">他信息发表任何形式的鉴证结论。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">结合我们对财务报表的审计，我们的责任是在能够获取上述其他</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">信息时阅读这些信息，在此过程中，考虑其他信息是否与财务报表或</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">我们在审计过程中了解到的情况存在重大不一致或者似乎存在重大错报。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">当我们阅读</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>X</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">报告后，如果确定其中存在重大错报，审计准则要求我们与治理层沟通该事项并采取</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">描述适用的措施</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -6.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-text-raise: 6.5pt'>8</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">（五）管理层和治理层对财务报表的责任</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1501</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">对财务报表形成审计意见和出具审计报告》的规定报告，见《</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&lt;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">中国注册会计师审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1501</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>对财务报表形成审计意见和出具审计报告<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&gt;</SPAN>应用<SPAN

face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN
