style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">年</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>月</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>日<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>5</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">：当注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取所有其他信息，并</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">且已确定其他信息存在重大错报时，适用于任何被审计单位，无论是</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">上市实体还是非上市实体的无保留意见审计报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>背景信息：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>．对上市实体或非上市实体整套财务报表进行审计。该审计不<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">属于集团审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">即不适用《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1401</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">对集团财务报表审计的特殊考虑》</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>．管理层按照企业会计准则编制财务报表；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">．审计业务约定条款体现了《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1111</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>就审计业务约定条款达成一致意见》中关于管理层对财务报表<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">责任的描述；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>．基于获取的审计证据，注册会计师认为发表无保留意见是恰当的；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>．适用的相关职业道德要求为中国注册会计师职业道德守则；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 15.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -2.6pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">．基于获取的审计证据，根据《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1324</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">持续经营》，注册会计师认为可能导致对被审计单位持续经营</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">能力产生重大疑虑的事项或情况不存在重大不确定性；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">．已按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>在审计报告<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">中沟通关键审计事项》的规定沟通了关键审计事项；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>8</SPAN>．注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取所有其他信息，并且已确定其他信息存在重大错报；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9</SPAN>．负责监督财务报表的人员与负责编制财务报表的人员不同；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">．除财务报表审计外，注册会计师不承担法律法规要求的其他</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">报告责任。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">审计报告</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>股份有限公司全体股东：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>一、审计意见<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt">我们审计了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">股份有限公司</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">以下简称</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">公司</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">财务报表，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">包括</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">日的资产负债表，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">年度的利润表、现金流</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">量表、股东权益变动表以及相关财务报表附注。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">我们认为，后附的财务报表在所有重大方面按照企业会计准则的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.15pt">规定编制，公允反映了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">公司</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">日的财务状况以及</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>20</FONT></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>年度的经营成果和现金流量。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">二、形成审计意见的基础</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">我们按照中国注册会计师审计准则的规定执行了审计工作。审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt">报告的</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt"><FONT face=微软雅黑>注册会计师对财务报表审计的责任</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">部分进一步阐述了我们</SPAN>在这些准则下的责任。按照中国注册会计师职业道德守则，我们独立<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.35pt">于</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">公司，并履行了职业道德方面的其他责任。我们相信，我们获取的审计证据是充分、适当的，为发表审计意见提供了基础。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>三、其他信息<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>公司管理层（以下简称管理层）对其他信息负责。其他信息包括<SPAN 
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[X</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">报告中涵盖的信息，但不包括财务报表和我们的审计报告</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">我们对财务报表发表的审计意见不涵盖其他信息，我们也不对其</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">他信息发表任何形式的鉴证结论。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>结合我们对财务报表的审计，我们的责任是阅读其他信息，在此<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">过程中，考虑其他信息是否与财务报表或我们在审计过程中了解到的</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>情况存在重大不一致或者似乎存在重大错报。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>基于我们已执行的工作，如果我们确定其他信息存在重大错报，我们应当报告该事实。如下所述，我们确定其他信息存在重大错报。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN>描述其他信息的重大错报<SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%"><FONT 
size=4>四、关键审计事项</FONT></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -6.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-width: 95%; mso-text-raise: 6.5pt'>9</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>关键审计事项是我们根据职业判断，认为对本期财务报表审计最<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">为重要的事项。这些事项的应对以对财务报表整体进行审计并形成审</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">计意见为背景，我们不对这些事项单独发表意见。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">在审计报告中沟</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">通关键审计事项》的规定描述每一关键审计事项。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">五、管理层和治理层对财务报表的责任</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1501</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">对财务报表形成审计意见和出具审计报告》的规定报告，见《</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&lt;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">中国注册会计师审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1501</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>对财务报表形成审计意见和出具审计报告<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&gt;</SPAN>应用<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">指南》参考格式</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">六、注册会计师对财务报表审计的责任</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1501</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">对财务报表形成审计意见和出具审计报告》的规定报告，见《</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&lt;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">中国注册会计师审计</SPAN><SPAN

style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1501</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>对财务报表形成审计意见和出具审计报告<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&gt;</SPAN>应用指南》参考格式<SPAN

style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN

style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -6.5pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-text-raise: 6.5pt'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US

<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>××</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>会计师事务所<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN

style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×××</SPAN><FONT

<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 6pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -4pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-text-raise: 4.0pt'>9</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">本段适用于按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>在审计报告中沟通关键审计事项》的规定沟通关键审计事项的情形。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 6pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -4pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-text-raise: 4.0pt'>10</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">如果被审计单位是非上市实体，需要参考《</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&lt;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1501</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">号<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>——</SPAN>对财务报表形成审计意见和出具审计报告</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&gt;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">应用指南》参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>11</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: 3.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-text-raise: -3.5pt">披露项目合伙人姓名的要求仅适用于上市实体。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>（盖章）<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 2">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN>（签名并盖章）中国注册会计<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">师</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.1pt">：</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -1.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×××</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>（签名并盖章）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>中国</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>××</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>市<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">年</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>月</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>日<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>6</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">：当注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取所有其他信息，但</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">合并财务报表重要项目的审计范围受到限制，且影响其他信息时，适</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">用于任何被审计单位，无论是上市实体还是非上市实体的保留意见审计报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>背景信息：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>．对上市实体或非上市实体整套合并财务报表进行审计。该审<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">计属于集团审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">即适用《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1401</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">对集团财务报表审计的特殊考虑》</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>．管理层按照</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>××</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">财务报告编制基础编制合并财务报表，该编制</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">基础允许被审计单位只列报合并财务报表；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">．审计业务约定条款体现了《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1111</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>就审计业务约定条款达成一致意见》中关于管理层对合并财务<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">报表责任的描述；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>．对于一项对境外关联方的投资，注册会计师无法获取充分、<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">适当的审计证据。无法获取充分、适当审计证据的可能影响对合并财</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">务报表而言被认为是重大但非广泛的</SPAN>（<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">即保留意见是适当的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>．适用的相关职业道德要求为中国注册会计师职业道德守则；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 15.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -2.6pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">．基于获取的审计证据，根据《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1324</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">持续经营》，注册会计师认为可能导致对被审计单位持续经营</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">能力产生重大疑虑的事项或情况不存在重大不确定性；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">．已按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>在审计报告<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">中沟通关键审计事项》的规定沟通了关键审计事项；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>8</SPAN>．注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取所有其他信息，且合并财务报表重要项目审计范围受到的限制也影响了其他信息；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9</SPAN>．负责监督合并财务报表的人员与负责编制合并财务报表的人员不同；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>10</SPAN>．除合并财务报表审计外，注册会计师不承担法律法规要求的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">其他报告责任。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">审计报告</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>股份有限公司全体股东：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>一、保留意见<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt">我们审计了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.8pt">股份有限公司及其子公司</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">以下简称</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>集团）<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">合并财务报表，包括</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt">日的合并资产负债表，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">度的合并利润表、合并现金流量表、合并股东权益变动表以及相关合</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">并财务报表附注。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.6pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt"><FONT face=微软雅黑>我们认为，除</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt"><FONT face=微软雅黑>形成保留意见的基础</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">部分所述事项可能产生的影</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">响外，后附的合并财务报表在所有重大方面按照</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -1.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>××</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">财务报告编制基础</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.05pt">的规定编制，公允反映了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">集团</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">日的合并财务状</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">况以及</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">年度的合并经营成果和合并现金流量。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">二、形成保留意见的基础</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">集团对本年度内取得的境外联营公司</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>XYZ</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">公司的投资以权</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">益法核算，截至</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">日，该项投资在合并资产负债表中的账面价值为</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>元，<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">集团按持股比例计算的</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>XYZ</SPAN>公司净收益份额</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">元已包含在集团本年度收益中。由于我们无法接触</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>XYZ</SPAN>公司的财<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.8pt">务信息、管理层以及注册会计师，我们无法就</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.9pt">集团对</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>XYZ</SPAN>公司<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.1pt">在</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.1pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.1pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">日投资的账面价值以及</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">集团按持股比例计算</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>的<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>XYZ</SPAN>公司当年度净收益份额获取充分、适当的审计证据。因此，我们无法确定是否需要对上述金额进行调整。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>我们按照中国注册会计师审计准则的规定执行了审计工作。审计报告的</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>注册会计师对合并财务报表审计的责任</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>部分进一步阐述了我们在这些准则下的责任。按照中国注册会计师职业道德守则，我们独立于<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>集团，并履行了职业道德方面的其他责任。我们相信，我们获取的审计证据是充分、适当的，为发表保留意见提供了基础。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>三、其他信息<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>集团管理层（以下简称管理层）对其他信息负责。其他信息包括<SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[X</SPAN>报告中涵盖的信息，但不包括合并财务报表和我们的审计报告<SPAN 
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">我们对合并财务报表发表的审计意见不涵盖其他信息，我们也不</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">对其他信息发表任何形式的鉴证结论。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>结合我们对合并财务报表的审计，我们的责任是阅读其他信息，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">在此过程中，考虑其他信息是否与合并财务报表或我们在审计过程中</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">了解到的情况存在重大不一致或者似乎存在重大错报。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>基于我们已执行的工作，如果我们确定其他信息存在重大错报，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">我们应当报告该事实。如上述</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt"><FONT face=微软雅黑>形成保留意见的基础</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">部分所述，我们</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.15pt">无法就</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.8pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.8pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">日</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.95pt">集团对</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>XYZ</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">公司投资的账面价值以</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 2pt">及</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">集团按持股比例计算的</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>XYZ</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">公司当年度净收益份额获取充分、</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">适当的审计证据。因此，我们无法确定与该事项相关的其他信息是否</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">存在重大错报。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>四、关键审计事项</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -6.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-text-raise: 6.5pt'>12</SPAN><SPAN

<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 6pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -4pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-text-raise: 4.0pt'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">本段适用于按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>在审计报告中沟通关键审计事项》的规定沟通关键审计事项的情形。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>关键审计事项是我们根据职业判断，认为对本期合并财务报表审<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">计最为重要的事项。这些事项的应对以对合并财务报表整体进行审计并形成审计意见为背景，我们不对这些事项单独发表意见。除</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>形成保留意见的基础</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>部分所述事项外，我们确定下列事项是需要在审计<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">报告中沟通的关键审计事项。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">在审计报告中沟</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">通关键审计事项》的规定描述每一关键审计事项。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>

<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 6pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -4pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-text-raise: 4.0pt'>13</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">如果被审计单位是非上市实体，需要参考《</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&lt;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1501</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">号<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>——</SPAN>对财务报表形成审计意见和出具审计报告</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>&gt;</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">应用指南》参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">，并进行适当改写。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>14</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: 3.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-text-raise: -3.5pt">披露项目合伙人姓名的要求仅适用于上市实体。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">参考格式</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>7</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">：当注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取所有其他信息，且</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">对合并财务报表发表的否定意见也对其他信息有影响时，适用于任何</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">被审计单位，无论是上市实体还是非上市实体的否定意见审计报告。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>背景信息：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>．对上市实体或非上市实体整套合并财务报表进行审计。该审<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">计属于集团审计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">即适用《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1401</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">对集团财务报表审计的特殊考虑》</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>．管理层按照</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>××</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">财务报告编制基础编制合并财务报表，该编制</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">基础允许被审计单位只列报合并财务报表；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">．审计业务约定条款体现了《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1111</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>就审计业务约定条款达成一致意见》中关于管理层对合并财务<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">报表责任的描述；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>．由于未合并一家子公司，合并财务报表存在重大错报，重大错报对合并财务报表而言被认为是广泛的（即否定意见是适当的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -6.9pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">由于不可行，合并财务报表错报的影响无法确定；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>．适用的相关职业道德要求为中国注册会计师职业道德守则；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 15.6pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -2.6pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">．基于获取的审计证据，根据《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1324</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">持续经营》，注册会计师认为可能导致对被审计单位持续经营</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">能力产生重大疑虑的事项或情况不存在重大不确定性；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">．已按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>在审计报告<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">中沟通关键审计事项》的规定沟通了关键审计事项；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>8</SPAN>．注册会计师在审计报告日前已获取所有其他信息，且对合并财务报表发表的否定意见也对其他信息有影响；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9</SPAN>．负责监督合并财务报表的人员与负责编制合并财务报表的人<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>员不同；<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.6pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>10</SPAN>．除合并财务报表审计外，注册会计师不承担法律法规要求的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">其他报告责任。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">审计报告</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>股份有限公司全体股东：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>一、否定意见<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt">我们审计了</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.8pt">股份有限公司及其子公司</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">以下简称</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>集团）<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">合并财务报表，包括</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt">日的合并资产负债表，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">年</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">度的合并利润表、合并现金流量表、合并股东权益变动表以及相关合</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">并财务报表附注。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>我们认为，由于</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>形成否定意见的基础</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>部分所述事项的重要性，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">后附的合并财务报表没有在所有重大方面按照</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -1.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>××</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">财务报告编制基础</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">的规定编制，未能公允反映</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">集团</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.75pt">年</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">月</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">日的合并财务</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">状况以及</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">年度的合并经营成果和合并现金流量。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-font-width: 95%">二、形成否定意见的基础</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 25.8pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt"><FONT face=微软雅黑>如财务报表附注</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">所述，由于无法确定</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.8pt">集团于</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>×</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>年度收购的子公司<SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>XYZ</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">公司某些重要资产和负债项目在收购日的公允价值，</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">集团未将该子公司纳入合并范围。该项投资以成本计量。根据</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -1.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>××</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>财务报告编制基础，<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>集团应将该子公司纳入合并范围，并以暂<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">估金额为基础核算该项收购。如果将</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>XYZ</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">公司纳入合并范围，后附</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">合并财务报表的多个项目将受到重大影响。我们尚未确定未将该公司</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">纳入合并范围对合并财务报表的影响。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>我们按照中国注册会计师审计准则的规定执行了审计工作。审计报告的</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>注册会计师对合并财务报表审计的责任</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>部分进一步阐述了我们在这些准则下的责任。按照中国注册会计师职业道德守则，我们独立于<SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>集团，并履行了职业道德方面的其他责任。我们相信，我们获取的审计证据是充分、适当的，为发表否定意见提供了基础。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>三、其他信息<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>集团管理层（以下简称管理层）对其他信息负责。其他信息包括<SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[X</SPAN>报告中涵盖的信息，但不包括合并财务报表和我们的审计报告<SPAN 
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.6pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">我们对合并财务报表发表的审计意见不涵盖其他信息，我们也不</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">对其他信息发表任何形式的鉴证结论。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>结合我们对合并财务报表的审计，我们的责任是阅读其他信息，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">在此过程中，考虑其他信息是否与合并财务报表或我们在审计过程中</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">了解到的情况存在重大不一致或者似乎存在重大错报。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>基于我们已执行的工作，如果我们确定其他信息存在重大错报，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">我们应当报告该事实。如上述</SPAN></FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt"><FONT face=微软雅黑>形成否定意见的基础</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt">部分所述，</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>ABC</SPAN>集团应当将<SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>XYZ</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">公司纳入合并范围，并以暂估金额为基础核算该项收购。我们认为，由于</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>X</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">报告中的相关金额或其他项目受到未合并</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>XYZ</SPAN>公司的影响，其他信息存在重大错报。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>四、关键审计事项</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -6.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-text-raise: 6.5pt'>15</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>关键审计事项是我们根据职业判断，认为对本期合并财务报表审<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">计最为重要的事项。这些事项的应对以对合并财务报表整体进行审计并形成审计意见为背景，我们不对这些事项单独发表意见。除</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>形成<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26pt"><o:wrapblock><v:line

<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 6pt; POSITION: relative; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TOP: -4pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-text-raise: 4.0pt'>15</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">本段适用于按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>在审计报告中沟通关键审计事项》的规定沟通关键审计事项的情形。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>否定意见的基础</FONT><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>部分所述事项外，我们确定下列事项是需要在审计报告中沟通的关键审计事项。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN>号</FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">在审计报告中沟</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">通关键审计事项》的规定描述每一关键审计事项。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">五、管理层和治理层对合并财务报表的责任</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT

style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>[</SPAN><SPAN

style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>]<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN

lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><FONT
